[[bf16-mode-switch-vector-widening-floating-point-add-subtract]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Widening Floating-Point Add/Subtract Intrinsics

[,c]
----
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwadd_vv_f32mf2(vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                                       size_t vl);

                                       size_t vl);

[[bf16-mode-switch-vector-floating-point-classify]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Floating-Point Classify Intrinsics

[,c]
----
vuint16mf4_t __riscv_vfclass_v_u16mf4(vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, size_t vl);
vuint16mf2_t __riscv_vfclass_v_u16mf2(vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, size_t vl);
vuint16m1_t __riscv_vfclass_v_u16m1(vbfloat16m1_t vs2, size_t vl);
vuint16m2_t __riscv_vfclass_v_u16m2(vbfloat16m2_t vs2, size_t vl);

// masked functions

                                        size_t vl);
vuint16mf2_t __riscv_vfclass_v_u16mf2_m(vbool32_t vm, vbfloat16mf2_t vs2,
                                        size_t vl);

                                      size_t vl);
vuint16m2_t __riscv_vfclass_v_u16m2_m(vbool8_t vm, vbfloat16m2_t vs2,
                                      size_t vl);

                                      size_t vl);

                                      size_t vl);
----
